***fata.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fata.html>fata</a> (47448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href = vnd.unilang:fata.html>fata</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fatōną</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:root.html>root</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ped-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:walk.html>walk</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:stumble.html>stumble</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:fall.html>fall</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nn">fatta</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:through.html>through</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaten.html>vaten</a></i>. <p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deliver.html>deliver</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fay.html>fay</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular <a href = vnd.unilang:simple.html>simple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">fays</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">faying</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:simple.html>simple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fayed.html>fayed</a></b>)

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>To</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fit.html>fit</a>.</li>
